```python
import json
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from matplotlib import pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import scipy.stats as stats
```


```python
park_point_data = []
with open('./data/Park_Label_Points___park_label_point.geojson', 'r') as parks_file:
    park_points = json.load(parks_file)
    for feature in park_points['features']:
        feature['properties'].update({'latitude': feature['geometry']['coordinates'][1], 'longitude': feature['geometry']['coordinates'][0]})
        feature[feature['properties']['OBJECTID']] = feature['properties']
        park_point_data.append(feature[feature['properties']['OBJECTID']])
    print(park_point_data)
```

```python
def json_lines(file):
    for line in file:
        if line.startswith('{') and len(line) > 2:
            line = line.rstrip(',\n')
            try:
                line = json.loads(line)
            except JSONDecodeError:
                continue 
            if len(np.shape(line['geometry']['coordinates'])) != 3:
                continue 
            long, lat = np.mean(np.array(line['geometry']['coordinates'][0]), axis=0)
            # result = str(len(np.shape(line['geometry']['coordinates']))) + '\n'
            line['properties'].update({'longitude':long, 'latitude': lat})
            result = json.dumps(line['properties']) + ',\n'
            yield result
```


```python
with open('./data/LCI_Opportunity_Area_Metrics___lci_opportunity_metrics_area.geojson') as lci_file:
    with open('./data/LCI_Parsed_with_Coordinates.json', 'w') as output:
        output.write('[\n')
        output.writelines(json_lines(lci_file))
        output.write(']')
        # for obj in range(300):

park_color = sns.color_palette(palette='Blues', as_cmap=True)
fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(20,18.25))
sns.scatterplot(data=census2020, x='longitude', y='latitude', hue='tree_pctle', s=2, palette=color, legend='brief')
sns.scatterplot(data=parks_data, x='longitude', y='latitude', color='.3', s=15, legend='brief')
plt.xlim(-122.585, -121.82)
plt.ylim(47.13, 47.81)
plt.show();
```


![png](output_10_0.png)
